             Service and Part Center - Serving Cherry Hill, Turnersville, &amp; Marlton Chevrolet Drivers
            </h3>
            <!-- -->
           </div>
           <div class="copy" model="subject" template="copy">
            Marlton and Cherry Hill Chevrolet drivers looking for their regular vehicle maintenance or considering upgrading any auto parts can visit our showroom in Westville. By choosing
            <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="52fb617d-d210-4b89-932d-2a5309dc5ecd" id="01481c0e-4112-4efd-bbba-700dc8e38650">

              our
             </gs>
            </gs>
            certified Chevy
            <a href="/Service" rel="external" target="_blank" title="">
             service
            </a>
            department, we are able to ensure that you're getting the right person for the right job. For as much as you care about your car and put in the time to make it your own, we will do the same with a great attention to detail. Marlton and Turnersville Chevrolet drivers can order
            <a href="/PartsOrderForm" rel="external" target="_blank" title="">
             parts
            </a>
            , accessories, and
            <a href="/TireFinder" rel="external" target="_blank" title="">
             tires
            </a>
            for all of their new and used vehicles. Now you can schedule your service
            <a href="/ServiceApptForm" rel="external" target="_blank" title="">
             appointment
            </a>
            online. So what are Cherry Hill drivers waiting for? Visit our Chevrolet showroom today!

       <div class="content">
        <div class="text">
         <div class="title" model="subject" template="title">
          <h2 if="title">
           Pellegrino Chevrolet in Westville - Serving Cherry Hill, Turnersville, &amp; Marlton Chevrolet Buyers
          </h2>
         </div>
         <div class="copy" model="subject" template="copy">
          Pellegrino Chevrolet welcomes Turnersville drivers to its showroom. As a regional Westville and Chevy dealer, also serving nearby Cherry Hill and Marlton Chevrolet lovers, we make it convenient for our customers to find the car, truck, or SUV they are looking for while offering exceptional customer service. Turnersville Chevrolet buyers can visit our showroom in Westville, located near Cherry Hill and Marlton areas and let our Chevrolet experts help them get into a new or used Chevy car, truck, or SUV that they wish to buy!
         </div>
         <div class="link" template="hyperlinks">
